[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Description[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Issue Type[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThis is a **dynamic-stack-buffer-overflow** vulnerability, specifically a [0m[1;36m4[0m[39m-byte [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mread operation that attempts to access memory beyond the bounds of a [0m               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mstack-allocated buffer.[0m                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Error Details[0m                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThe overflow occurs at address `[0m[1;36m0x7ffede4397bc[0m[39m` in thread T0, where the program [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mattempts to read [0m[1;36m4[0m[39m bytes from a location that falls within the right alloca redzone[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;39m([0m[39mindicated by the shadow byte value `cb`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m. The shadow memory analysis shows:[0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Address `[0m[1;36m0x7ffede4397bc[0m[39m` is marked as `[0m[1;39m[[0m[39mcb[0m[1;39m][0m[39m` [0m[1;39m([0m[39mRight alloca redzone[0m[1;39m)[0m               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- The bytes immediately before this address are also marked as `cb` [0m[1;39m([0m[39mRight alloca [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mredzone[0m[1;39m)[0m                                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- The overflow indicates an out-of-bounds read operation on a dynamically allocated[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mstack buffer[0m                                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m665[0m[39m:    float uspill_image[0m[1;39m[[0m[39mimage->width[0m[1;39m][0m[1;39m[[0m[39mimage->height[0m[1;39m][0m[39m;[0m                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m666[0m[39m:    float vspill_image[0m[1;39m[[0m[39mimage->width[0m[1;39m][0m[1;39m[[0m[39mimage->height[0m[1;39m][0m[39m;[0m                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mcode[0m[39m>[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<code>[0m                                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39msrc/reformat.[0m[1;92mc:786[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m793[0m                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m786[0m[39m:                    uspill_image[0m[1;39m[[0m[39mi[0m[1;39m][0m[1;39m[[0m[39mj[0m[1;39m][0m[39m -= spill_Cb;[0m                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m787[0m[39m:                    vspill_image[0m[1;39m[[0m[39mi[0m[1;39m][0m[1;39m[[0m[39mj[0m[1;39m][0m[39m -= spill_Cr;[0m                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m788[0m[39m:                    uspill_image[0m[1;39m[[0m[39mi+adjCol[0m[1;39m][0m[1;39m[[0m[39mj[0m[1;39m][0m[39m += pSpillCb;[0m                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m789[0m[39m:                    vspill_image[0m[1;39m[[0m[39mi+adjCol[0m[1;39m][0m[1;39m[[0m[39mj[0m[1;39m][0m[39m += pSpillCr;[0m                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m790[0m[39m:                    uspill_image[0m[1;39m[[0m[39mi[0m[1;39m][0m[1;39m[[0m[39mj+adjRow[0m[1;39m][0m[39m += pSpillCb;[0m                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m791[0m[39m:                    vspill_image[0m[1;39m[[0m[39mi[0m[1;39m][0m[1;39m[[0m[39mj+adjRow[0m[1;39m][0m[39m += pSpillCr;[0m                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m792[0m[39m:                    uspill_image[0m[1;39m[[0m[39mi+adjCol[0m[1;39m][0m[1;39m[[0m[39mj+adjRow[0m[1;39m][0m[39m += pSpillCb;[0m               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m793[0m[39m:                    vspill_image[0m[1;39m[[0m[39mi+adjCol[0m[1;39m][0m[1;39m[[0m[39mj+adjRow[0m[1;39m][0m[39m += pSpillCr;[0m               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mcode[0m[39m>[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<code>[0m                                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39msrc/reformat.[0m[1;92mc:810[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m817[0m                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m810[0m[39m:                        uspill_image[0m[1;39m[[0m[39mi[0m[1;39m][0m[1;39m[[0m[39mj[0m[1;39m][0m[39m -= pSpillCb;[0m                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m811[0m[39m:                        vspill_image[0m[1;39m[[0m[39mi[0m[1;39m][0m[1;39m[[0m[39mj[0m[1;39m][0m[39m -= pSpillCb;[0m                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m812[0m[39m:                        uspill_image[0m[1;39m[[0m[39mi+a[0m[1;39m][0m[1;39m[[0m[39mj[0m[1;39m][0m[39m -= pSpillCb;[0m                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m813[0m[39m:                        vspill_image[0m[1;39m[[0m[39mi+a[0m[1;39m][0m[1;39m[[0m[39mj[0m[1;39m][0m[39m -= pSpillCr;[0m                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m814[0m[39m:                        uspill_image[0m[1;39m[[0m[39mi[0m[1;39m][0m[1;39m[[0m[39mj+b[0m[1;39m][0m[39m -= pSpillCb;[0m                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m815[0m[39m:                        vspill_image[0m[1;39m[[0m[39mi[0m[1;39m][0m[1;39m[[0m[39mj+b[0m[1;39m][0m[39m -= pSpillCr;[0m                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m816[0m[39m:                        uspill_image[0m[1;39m[[0m[39mi+a[0m[1;39m][0m[1;39m[[0m[39mj+b[0m[1;39m][0m[39m -= pSpillCb;[0m                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m817[0m[39m:                        vspill_image[0m[1;39m[[0m[39mi+a[0m[1;39m][0m[1;39m[[0m[39mj+b[0m[1;39m][0m[39m -= pSpillCr;[0m                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mcode[0m[39m>[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mcode_snippets[0m[39m>[0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Fix Strategy[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<fix_strategy>[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Analysis of the Issue[0m                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mAfter examining the code snippets and the evaluation report, I have identified the [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mroot cause of the dynamic-stack-buffer-overflow vulnerability:[0m                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Root Cause[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThe vulnerability occurs in the `avifImageYUVAnyToRGBAnySlow` function at [0m          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`[0m[35m/src/libavif/src/[0m[95mreformat.c[0m[39m`, specifically in the chroma spill dampening code path[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;39m([0m[39mlines [0m[1;36m798[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m818[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m. The code calculates offset variables `a` and `b` to access [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mneighboring pixels in the `uspill_image` and `vspill_image` arrays but fails to [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mperform bounds checking before using these offsets for array access.[0m                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Key Findings[0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. **Stack-allocated arrays**: Lines [0m[1;36m665[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m666[0m[39m declare VLA arrays [0m                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`uspill_image[0m[1;39m[[0m[39mimage->width[0m[1;39m][0m[1;39m[[0m[39mimage->height[0m[1;39m][0m[39m` and [0m                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`vspill_image[0m[1;39m[[0m[39mimage->width[0m[1;39m][0m[1;39m[[0m[39mimage->height[0m[1;39m][0m[39m` on the stack.[0m                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. **Inconsistent bounds checking**: [0m                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Lines [0m[1;36m774[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m782[0m[39m calculate `adjCol` and `adjRow` with proper bounds checking[0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Lines [0m[1;36m800[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m809[0m[39m calculate `a` and `b` with the SAME pattern but WITHOUT bounds [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mchecking[0m                                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - This inconsistency is the direct cause of the buffer overflow[0m                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. **Vulnerable array accesses**: Lines [0m[1;36m812[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m817[0m[39m access the arrays with unchecked [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39moffsets:[0m                                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - `uspill_image[0m[1;39m[[0m[39mi+a[0m[1;39m][0m[1;39m[[0m[39mj[0m[1;39m][0m[39m` where `a` can be [0m[1;36m-1[0m[39m or [0m[1;36m1[0m                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - `uspill_image[0m[1;39m[[0m[39mi[0m[1;39m][0m[1;39m[[0m[39mj+b[0m[1;39m][0m[39m` where `b` can be [0m[1;36m-1[0m[39m or [0m[1;36m1[0m                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - `uspill_image[0m[1;39m[[0m[39mi+a[0m[1;39m][0m[1;39m[[0m[39mj+b[0m[1;39m][0m[39m` combining both risks[0m                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. **Out-of-bounds scenarios**:[0m                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - When `[0m[33mi[0m[39m=[0m[1;36m0[0m[39m` and `[0m[33ma[0m[39m=[0m[1;36m-1[0m[39m`: negative index access[0m                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - When `[0m[33mi[0m[39m=[0m[35mwidth[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m1[0m[39m` and `[0m[33ma[0m[39m=[0m[1;36m1[0m[39m`: exceeds array bounds[0m                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Same issues for `j` dimension with `b`[0m                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Fix Strategy[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Step [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m: Add bounds checking for variables `a` and `b`[0m                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mInsert bounds checking code immediately after lines [0m[1;36m800[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m809[0m[39m where `a` and `b` are [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcalculated, and before lines [0m[1;36m810[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m817[0m[39m where they are used for array access.[0m          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThe bounds checking should follow this pattern:[0m                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mAfter calculating a and b [0m[1;39m([0m[39mafter line [0m[1;36m809[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m:[0m                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Check if i + a would be out of bounds [0m[1;39m([0m[39m< [0m[1;36m0[0m[39m or >= image->width[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, set a = [0m[1;36m0[0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Check if j + b would be out of bounds [0m[1;39m([0m[39m< [0m[1;36m0[0m[39m or >= image->height[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, set b = [0m[1;36m0[0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mSince `i` and `j` are unsigned integers [0m[1;39m([0m[39muint32_t[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, we need to handle both [0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39munderflow and overflow cases properly:[0m                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- For underflow: Check if the offset is negative and the index is at the boundary [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;39m([0m[39mi.e., `a < [0m[1;36m0[0m[39m && i == [0m[1;36m0[0m[39m`[0m[1;39m)[0m                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- For overflow: Check if the resulting index would exceed the array bounds [0m[1;39m([0m[39mi.e., [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`i + a >= image->width`[0m[1;39m)[0m                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Step [0m[1;36m2[0m[39m: Implementation approach[0m                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mAdd the following bounds checking logic after line [0m[1;36m809[0m[39m and before line [0m[1;36m810[0m[39m:[0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```c[0m                                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m Bounds checking for a [0m[1;39m([0m[39mcolumn offset[0m[1;39m)[0m                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mif [0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m([0m[39ma < [0m[1;36m0[0m[39m && i == [0m[1;36m0[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m || [0m[1;39m([0m[39ma > [0m[1;36m0[0m[39m && i >= image->width - [0m[1;36m1[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    a = [0m[1;36m0[0m[39m;[0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;39m}[0m                                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m Bounds checking for b [0m[1;39m([0m[39mrow offset[0m[1;39m)[0m                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mif [0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m([0m[39mb < [0m[1;36m0[0m[39m && j == [0m[1;36m0[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m || [0m[1;39m([0m[39mb > [0m[1;36m0[0m[39m && j >= image->height - [0m[1;36m1[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    b = [0m[1;36m0[0m[39m;[0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;39m}[0m                                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThis pattern:[0m                                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. Handles negative offsets when at the left/top boundary [0m[1;39m([0m[39msets offset to [0m[1;36m0[0m[1;39m)[0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. Handles positive offsets when at the right/bottom boundary [0m[1;39m([0m[39msets offset to [0m[1;36m0[0m[1;39m)[0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. Mirrors the logic used for `adjCol` and `adjRow` at lines [0m[1;36m777[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m782[0m                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. Ensures all array accesses at lines [0m[1;36m810[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m817[0m[39m remain within valid bounds[0m           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Step [0m[1;36m3[0m[39m: Verification of the fix[0m                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThe fix ensures that:[0m                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- All accesses `uspill_image[0m[1;39m[[0m[39mi+a[0m[1;39m][0m[1;39m[[0m[39mj[0m[1;39m][0m[39m` are safe because `a` will be [0m[1;36m0[0m[39m if out of [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mbounds[0m                                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- All accesses `uspill_image[0m[1;39m[[0m[39mi[0m[1;39m][0m[1;39m[[0m[39mj+b[0m[1;39m][0m[39m` are safe because `b` will be [0m[1;36m0[0m[39m if out of [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mbounds[0m                                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- All accesses `uspill_image[0m[1;39m[[0m[39mi+a[0m[1;39m][0m[1;39m[[0m[39mj+b[0m[1;39m][0m[39m` are safe because both offsets are validated[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- The dampening logic still functions correctly for interior pixels[0m                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Edge pixels are handled gracefully by not applying neighbor dampening[0m             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Justification[0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Why this is optimal:[0m                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. **Minimal change**: Only adds [0m[1;36m6[0m[39m lines of bounds checking code[0m                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. **Consistent with existing code**: Uses the same pattern as `adjCol`[0m[35m/[0m[39m`adjRow` [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mchecking at lines [0m[1;36m777[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m782[0m                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. **Preserves functionality**: The dampening logic remains active for all valid [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mpixel positions[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. **No performance impact**: Only adds simple conditional checks in an already [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mconditional code path[0m                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m5[0m[39m. **Defensive programming**: Prevents undefined behavior from out-of-bounds array [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39maccess[0m                                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### How it preserves existing logic:[0m                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- The dampening algorithm still works for interior pixels where neighbor access is [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mvalid[0m                                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Edge pixels gracefully skip neighbor dampening by setting offsets to [0m[1;36m0[0m            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- The spill accumulation and threshold logic [0m[1;39m([0m[39mline [0m[1;36m798[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m remains unchanged[0m           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- The array initialization [0m[1;39m([0m[39mlines [0m[1;36m669[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m674[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m remains unchanged[0m                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- The main conversion logic outside this code path is unaffected[0m                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### How it addresses the evaluation report:[0m                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Directly fixes the buffer overflow at line [0m[1;36m812[0m[39m mentioned in the report[0m            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Prevents similar overflows at lines [0m[1;36m813[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m817[0m                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Addresses both underflow [0m[1;39m([0m[39mnegative indices[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m and overflow [0m[1;39m([0m[39mexceeds bounds[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mscenarios[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- The fix is in the exact location identified by the stack trace[0m                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Potential side effects and mitigation:[0m                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- **Side effect**: Edge pixels will not have neighbor dampening applied[0m             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- **Mitigation**: This is actually correct behavior - edge pixels don't have all [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mneighbors, so dampening should only affect their own spill values, which still [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mhappens at lines [0m[1;36m810[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m811[0m                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- **No breaking changes**: The fix doesn't modify function signatures, return [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mvalues, or the overall conversion pipeline[0m                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- **No impact on other code paths**: The fix is isolated to the [0m                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mAVIF_CHROMA_UPSAMPLING_SPILL path for YUV420 format[0m                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Similar patterns in the codebase:[0m                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThe bounds checking pattern used here directly mirrors the existing pattern at [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mlines [0m[1;36m777[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m782[0m[39m for `adjCol` and `adjRow`, and is similar to the comprehensive edge [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mhandling at lines [0m[1;36m912[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m939[0m[39m in the main upsampling code. This demonstrates that the [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mfix follows established best practices already present in the codebase.[0m             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
